# Files Missing Proper YAML Front Matter Descriptions

This document lists all .md files in the repository that do not have a proper description in their YAML front matter.

## Requirements

Each .md file should have a description in the YAML front matter that:
- Starts with `description: `
- Is between 100 and 150 characters in length

## Summary

- **Total files needing fixes: 6,415**
  - Files with no description: 6,413
  - Files with description too short (<100 chars): 1
  - Files with description too long (>150 chars): 1
